        <script type="text/javascript">
    //<!--
    
	$(document).ready(function(){
        var count = 0; 
        var self = this;
        $.ajax({
            url: path+'/programacao/get-twitter',
            type: 'GET',
            success: function(response){
               var tweets = response;
               if(tweets.length <= 0 || tweetPermission == 'disable'){
                $('.right-feed').hide();
               }else{
                   updateTweets(tweets, count);
                   count += 4;
                   if(count >= tweets.length-1) count = 0;

                   setInterval(function(){

                       updateTweets(tweets, count);
                       count += 4;
                       //if(count >= tweets.length-1) count = 0;
                   }, 15000);               
               }
            }
        });
        
     function updateTweets(tweets, count){
        var list = '';
        var self = this;
        for(var i = 0; i < 3 ; i++){  
           if(tweets[count] && tweets[count].text != undefined){
               var tweet = "<div class='feed-item'><b>"+tweets[count].from_user_name+"</b>"+tweets[count].text+"</div>";
               list += tweet;
               count++;
           }
       }
       if(list != ''){ 
            TweenLite.to($('.right-feed .feed-item'), 0.4, {css: {opacity:'0'}, ease:Expo.easeInOut, onComplete: function(){
                var pai = $('.right-feed');
                $(pai).html('').append('<div class="feed-header">Agora no Twitter</div>').append(list).fadeIn();
                TweenLite.to($('.right-feed .feed-item'), 0.4, {css: {opacity:'1'}, ease:Expo.easeInOut});                
            }});          
    
       } 
     }
